<h2>PMAG&nbsp;30 AR/M4 GEN M2 MOE, 5.56x45 Magazine</h2> <p><font face="book antiqua,palatino" size="3"><span>The PMAG 30 AR/M4 GEN M2 MOE is a 30-round 5.56x45 NATO (.223 Remington) AR15/M4 compatible magazine that offers a cost competitive upgrade from the aluminum USGI. It features an impact resistant polymer construction, easy to disassemble design with a flared floorplate for positive magazine extraction, resilient stainless steel spring for corrosion resistance, and an anti-tilt, self-lubricating follower for increased reliability.</span></font><br><br><font face="book antiqua,palatino" size="3"><span>The GEN M2 MOE is identical in form and function to the older model PMAG except that the optional Impact/Dust Cover is now sold separately.&nbsp;</span></font><br><br><font face="book antiqua,palatino" size="3"><span>Made in U.S.A.</span></font></p> <p><span><img src="../../../../Data/Default/Images/uploads/magpul/magpul-mag571-blk-873750008264-2.jpg" alt="" width="540" height="588"></span></p> <p><span><font face="book antiqua,palatino" size="3"><span>Magpul Original Equipment (MOE) is a line of firearm accessories designed to provide a high-quality, economical alternative to standard weapon parts. The MOE line distinguishes itself with a simplified feature set, but maintains Magpul engineering and material quality.</span></font><br></span></p></span></div> </div><div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_TabSpecifications" class="ajax__tab_panel" style="display:none;visibility:hidden;"> <div class="Features"> <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_TabSpecifications_ProductsSpecifications"><strong>Features</strong><p></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <p>&nbsp;</p> <ul> <li>Impact and crush resistant polymer construction</li> <li>Constant-curve internal geometry for smooth feeding</li> <li>Anti-tilt, self-lubricating follower for increased reliability</li> <li>USGI-spec stainless steel spring for corrosion resistance and field compatibility</li> <li>Textured gripping surface and flared floorplate for positive magazine handling and easy disassembly</li> </ul></span></div> </div><div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews" class="ajax__tab_panel" style="display:none;visibility:hidden;"> <div class="Reviews"> <div id="Review"> <div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews_uxProductReviews_UpdatePnlProductReviewDetails"> <div class="Sorting"> <span class="TitleStyle"> Reviewed by <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlCustomerReviews_uxProductReviews_CustomersCnt">2</span> customer </span>&nbsp; I was having problems with my older AR-15 Colt brand metal magazines with the regular round bullet type follower always misfeeding or double feeding on the last 2 rounds due to tilting. This magazine with it's box type follower and anti-tilt system eliminated my feeding problems. Bullets lay completely flat on the follower all the way through the last round. Planning on buying a few more of these. These are also easy to take apart for cleaning. Just push a button and slide the base plate out.</div> <div class="Row"> By <span class="Text"> Amp</span> from <span class="Text"> Salt Lake City</span></div> </div> </div> </td> </tr><tr> <td class="ReviewItem"> <div class="ItemStyle"> <div class="Title"> <span class="Subject"> Best magazine oit there</span>, June 09, 2013</div> <div class="Content"> <div class="StarRating"> <img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"><img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"><img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"><img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"><img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"></div> <div class="Row"> Absolutely flawless product.
